    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">رَكَبَ</orth>
                  </form>, (A, K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">رُكُوبٌ</foreign> (S, A, K) and <foreign lang="ar">مَرْكَبٌ</foreign>; (A, K;) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-1" target="ارتكبهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>; (K;) <hi rend="ital">I. q.</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عَلَاهُ</foreign> (A, K, TA) and <foreign lang="ar">عَلَا عَلَيْهِ</foreign> [explained by what follows]. (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبْتُ الدَّابَّةَ</foreign>, (Msb,) or <foreign lang="ar">الفَرَسَ</foreign>, (Mgh,) and <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبْتُ عَلَيْهَا</foreign>, [or <foreign lang="ar">عَلَيْهِ</foreign>,] inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">رُكُوبٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَرْكَبٌ</foreign> [as above, meaning <hi rend="ital">I rode,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">rode upon,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">I mounted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mounted upon, the beast,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the horse</hi>]. (TA. [See also <foreign lang="ar">رَاكِبٌ</foreign>.]) [And <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبْتُ السَّفِينَةَ</foreign>, or <foreign lang="ar">فِى السَّفِينَةِ</foreign> (agreeably with the Kur xi. 43 and xviii. 70 and xxix. 65), <hi rend="ital">I embarked in the ship; went on board the ship.</hi>] And one says, of anything, <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَهُ</foreign> [and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-2" target="ارتكبه" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>] as meaning <foreign lang="ar">عَلَاهُ</foreign> [i. e. <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">It was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, upon,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">over, it; got upon it; came,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">arose, upon it; overlay it; was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, superincumbent,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">supernatant, upon it; overspread it</hi>]; namely, another thing. (TA.) [In like manner,] one says also, of anything, <foreign lang="ar">رُكِبَ</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-3" target="اُرْتُكِبَ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> as meaning <foreign lang="ar">عُلِىَ</foreign> [i. e., when said of a horse or the like, <hi rend="ital">He was ridden,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">ridden upon,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">was mounted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mounted upon:</hi> whence other significations in other cases, indicated above]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ بَعْضُهُ بَعْضًا</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">i. q.</hi>   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-4" target="تراكب" n="4" type="1" subtype="SO" lang="ar" select="n16455"/></foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">It lay one part upon another; it was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, heaped,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">piled, up,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">together, one part upon,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">overlying, another:</hi>] said of fat [as meaning <hi rend="ital">it was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, disposed in layers, one above another:</hi> see <foreign lang="ar">رَاكِبَةٌ</foreign>]. (A, TA.) [And hence, <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ النَّاسُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">The people bore,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">pressed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">crowded,</hi> (<hi rend="ital">as though mounting,</hi>) <hi rend="ital">one upon another;</hi> a phrase well known, and of frequent occurrence: or meaning <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">the people followed one another closely;</hi> from what next follows.]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَهُ</foreign> also means [<assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He came upon him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">overtook him;</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">he followed closely,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">immediately, after him:</hi> and <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبْتُ أَثَرَهُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">طَرِيقَهُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">I followed close after him.</hi> (L.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  [<foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ الطَّرِيقَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">الرَّمْلَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">المَفَازَةَ</foreign>, <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He went upon,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">trod,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">travelled, the road,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">the sand</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sands, and the desert:</hi> and <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ البَحْرَ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He embarked,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">voyaged, upon the sea.</hi> Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ اللَّيْلَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">الهَوْلَ</foreign>, <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">He ventured upon, encountered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">braved, the night,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">that which was terrible</hi> or <hi rend="ital">fearful,</hi>] and the like thereof. (TA.) [And <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ أَمْرًا</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-5" target="ارتكبهُ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He ventured upon, embarked in,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">undertook, an affair:</hi> and <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">he surmounted it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mastered it:</hi> the former meaning is well known: the latter is indicated by an explanation of the phrase <foreign lang="ar">رَكَّابٌ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">لِلْأُمُورِ</foreign>, which see below.] And <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ ذَنْبًا</foreign> (A, K) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-6" target="ارتكبهُ" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> (S, A, MA, K) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">He committed a sin,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">crime,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like.</hi> (S, MA, TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">فُلَانٌ فُلَانًا بِأَمْرٍ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Such a one did to such a one a thing</hi>]. (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَهُ بِمَكْرُوهٍ</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-7" target="ارتكبهُ" n="7" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">He did to him an evil,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">abominable,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">odious, deed</hi>]. (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبْتُ الدَّيْنَ</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-8" target="ارتكبتهُ" n="8" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">I became much in debt:</hi> and <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَنِى الدَّيْنُ</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n16451-9" target="ارتكبنى" n="9" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Debt burdened me</hi>]. (Msb.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">رَكِبَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">رَأْسَهُ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">He went at random, heedlessly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">in a headlong manner,</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">مَضَى عَلَى وَجْهِهِ</foreign>, A, Msb,) [i. e.,] <hi rend="ital">without consideration,</hi> (A,) or <hi rend="ital">without any certain aim,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">object,</hi> (Msb,) <hi rend="ital">not obeying a guide to the right course.</hi> (A.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">يُرْكَبُ رَأْسَهُ لَا</foreign>

                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">رُكْبَةٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> a word of well-known meaning, (S, Msb,) [The <hi rend="ital">knee;</hi> i. e., in a man,] the <hi rend="ital">joint between the lower parts of the thigh and the upper parts of the shank:</hi> (A, K:) or [in a quadruped,] the <hi rend="ital">joint between the metacarpus and the radius</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">مَوْصِلُ الوَظِيفِ وَالذِّرَاعِ</foreign>): this is the right explanation: in the K, <foreign lang="ar">مَوْضِع</foreign> is erroneously put for <foreign lang="ar">مَوْصِل</foreign>: [this explanation is evidently given accord. to the terms employed in the anatomy of quadrupeds as compared to human beings: in that which next follows, there is certainly an omission, which I have endeavoured to supply:] or the <foreign lang="ar">رُكْبَتَانِ</foreign> of the fore legs of the camel are the <hi rend="ital">two joints that</hi> [<hi rend="ital">project forwards, in like manner as do, in the hind legs, those that</hi>] <hi rend="ital">are next the belly</hi> [meaning <hi rend="ital">the stifle-joints</hi>] <hi rend="ital">when he lies down upon his breast with folded legs:</hi> the two joints that project behind [in the hind legs, namely, the hocks,] are called the <foreign lang="ar">عُرْقُوبَانِ</foreign>: in every quadruped, the <foreign lang="ar">ركبتان</foreign> are in the fore legs, and the <foreign lang="ar">عرقوبان</foreign> are in the hind legs: and the <foreign lang="ar">عرقوب</foreign> is what is called <foreign lang="ar">مَوْصِلُ الوَظِيفِ</foreign> [i. e. the upper joint of the metatarsus]: (TA:) or the <foreign lang="ar">ركبة</foreign> is the <foreign lang="ar">مِرْفَق</foreign> [which in a man is the elbow, but here seems to mean the <hi rend="ital">lower joint</hi>] <hi rend="ital">of the</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ذِرَاع</foreign> [or <hi rend="ital">radius</hi>] of anything [i. e. of any beast]: (K:) [from its being said in the S and Msb that the <foreign lang="ar">رُكْبَة</foreign> is “ well known, ” I conclude that there is no real discrepancy in the foregoing explanations: it is perhaps needless to add that the term <foreign lang="ar">رُكْبَة</foreign> is now universally applied to the <hi rend="ital">knee</hi> of a man and to what we commonly call the <hi rend="ital">knee</hi> of a horse and the like:] the pl. is <foreign lang="ar">رُكَبٌ</foreign>, (S, Msb, K,) i. e. the pl. of mult., and the pl. of pauc. is <foreign lang="ar">رُكْبَاتٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">رُكَبَاتٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">رُكُبَاتٌ</foreign>.
